# E2R Stock-Web Historical Calibration / Sector-Archetype Residual Research Round

## 0. Research Metadata

```text
mode = historical_trigger_level_calibration_after_stock_web_ohlc_breakthrough_v12
research_session = post_calibrated_sector_archetype_residual_research
round = R13
loop = 14
large_sector_id = L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC
canonical_archetype_id = C31_POLICY_SUBSIDY_LEGISLATION_EVENT
fine_archetype_id = BATCH_PROMOTION_REVIEW_CROSS_SECTOR_SHADOW_LEDGER
output_file = e2r_stock_web_v12_residual_round_R13_loop_14_L10_POLICY_EVENT_CROSS_REDTEAM_MISC_C31_POLICY_SUBSIDY_LEGISLATION_EVENT_research.md
production_scoring_changed = false
shadow_weight_only = true
handoff_prompt_embedded = true
handoff_prompt_executed_now = false
```

This loop is a **batch promotion review** over the v12 residual MD corpus already produced in this session. It does not add live candidates, does not patch `stock_agent`, and does not change production scoring. It aggregates the local v12 MD rows to decide which sector/canonical-archetype shadow rules are ready for a later implementation batch and which should remain watch-only.

## 1. Current Calibrated Profile Assumption

```text
current_default_profile_proxy = e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated
previous_baseline_reference = e2r_2_0_baseline
stage2_actionable_evidence_bonus = +2.0
stage3_yellow_total_min = 75.0
stage3_green_total_min = 87.0
stage3_green_revision_min = 55.0
stage3_cross_evidence_green_buffer = +1.5
price_only_blowoff_blocks_positive_stage = true
full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence = true
hard_4c_thesis_break_routes_to_4c = true
```

The batch review treats these axes as the current floor, not as discoveries. The question is whether the v12 holdouts justify **sector/canonical-archetype shadow ledgers** that are more specific than the global rules.

## 12. Trigger-Level OHLC Backtest Tables

Representative trigger averages by canonical group are embedded in the coverage matrix above. All underlying trigger rows with entry price, MFE/MAE, peak, drawdown, 4B local/full proximity, and current-profile verdict are emitted in JSONL in section 25.

## 13. Current Calibrated Profile Stress Test

Batch verdict: the calibrated profile improved global discipline, but residual errors cluster by archetype. The largest recurring residuals are:

- **False positives from event/theme/control premium without conversion bridge.** This appears in biotech binary events, content IP event premiums, software/security theme moves, policy subsidy cases, and governance/tender caps.
- **Too-late structural recognition when the bridge is non-standard but visible.** Examples include channel reorder in consumer exports, CSM/reserve quality in insurance, owned-traffic ad leverage, and named HBM equipment order routes.
- **4B too early when price-only local peaks are treated as full-cycle exhaustion.** The local/full-window split repeatedly shows that full 4B needs non-price deterioration or explicit cap evidence.
- **4C too late in binary/legal/PF/control cases.** Hard negative evidence should trigger faster 4C watch at the archetype level, while still avoiding price-only 4C.

## 14. Stage2 / Yellow / Green Comparison

The batch does not re-propose the global Stage2 bonus, Yellow threshold, or Green threshold. It keeps them as tested axes and adds only archetype-specific interpretation: Green promotion should require the **right bridge** for the archetype, not merely total score plus price momentum. Where the bridge is absent, Yellow/watch or 4B overlay is preferred even if price strength is high.

## 15. 4B Local vs Full-window Timing Audit

The corpus supports keeping `full_4b_requires_non_price_evidence`. The refinement is not global: each archetype needs its own acceptable non-price 4B evidence vocabulary. Examples: revision/delivery slowdown for HBM equipment; channel or margin slowdown for consumer exports; event-cap proximity for governance/tender; legal/PF break for construction; margin/backlog slowdown for software/security.

## 16. 4C Protection Audit

Hard 4C routing remains useful but timing should be sharpened in high-binary archetypes. The batch recommends fast 4C watch where trial/regulatory, legal/PF, tender/control, policy conversion, or accounting/trust evidence directly breaks the thesis.

## 18. Canonical-Archetype Rule Candidate

Batch-level shadow rule families:

1. `bridge_required_family`: before Green/promotion, require the appropriate non-price bridge for the canonical archetype: customer-named order, backlog, channel reorder, margin bridge, CSM/reserve quality, cash conversion, reimbursement revenue, or retained SaaS/security contract quality.
2. `event_premium_cap_family`: binary approval/trial, policy subsidy, control premium, and content IP event spikes should be capped unless cashflow conversion is visible by the trigger date.
3. `full_4b_specificity_family`: price-only local peaks stay overlay-only; full 4B requires non-price deterioration/cap evidence that is meaningful for the archetype.
4. `hard_4c_fast_route_family`: thesis-break evidence in binary/legal/PF/tender/policy archetypes should enter 4C watch quickly, but still not from price alone.

## 19. Before / After Backtest Comparison

No production score is recomputed. The after-profile is a shadow-only ledger recommendation. The observed aggregate direction is that more specific bridge gates would reduce `current_profile_false_positive` rows, while 4B specificity would reduce early full-exit errors without weakening the global guardrail.

## 23. Validation Scope / Non-Validation Scope

Validation scope: local v12 MD rows generated using stock-web OHLC, their case/trigger/score_simulation/residual rows, and stock-web source metadata. Non-validation scope: no live stock discovery, no broker API, no new price route, no production code, no final investment recommendation, and no direct global scoring promotion.

## 24. Shadow Weight Calibration

The batch proposes only shadow ledger acceptance priorities. It explicitly does not change production scoring.

|axis|scope|canonical_scope|confidence|proposal_type|notes|
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
|bridge_required_family|canonical_archetype_specific|C07|C09|C18|C20|C23|C25|C26|C27|C28|C29|C31|C32|medium|batch_shadow_ledger_only|No production delta; promote into sector/archetype shadow ledger for later implementation review.|

|full_4b_requires_revision_delivery_or_margin_slowdown|canonical_archetype_specific|C07|C09|C18|C20|C25|C26|C27|C28|C29|C30|C31|C32|medium|batch_shadow_ledger_only|Existing global guard kept; this only refines sector/archetype evidence taxonomy.|

## 26. Deferred Coding Agent Handoff Prompt

### Purpose

You are now in the repository implementation phase. The attached Markdown files are v12 post-calibrated residual research outputs produced using the Songdaiki/stock-web OHLC atlas.

These MDs are not live candidate research. They are historical calibration research designed to extend the already-applied e2r_2_1_stock_web_calibrated profile.

Do not blindly apply every shadow row. Ingest the machine-readable rows and update the sector/canonical-archetype calibration ledger.

### Price source context

- Primary historical price source used by the research MD: Songdaiki/stock-web.
- Price basis: tradable_raw.
- Price adjustment status: raw_unadjusted_marcap.
- Price shard pattern: atlas/ohlcv_tradable_by_symbol_year/<prefix>/<ticker>/<year>.csv.
- Symbol profile pattern: atlas/symbol_profiles/<prefix>/<ticker>.json.

### Rules

- Use only calibration_usable=true rows for quantitative calibration.
- Do not count reused cases as new independent evidence unless independent_evidence_weight > 0.
- Do not treat schema_rematerialization_only or duplicate_low_value_loop as new evidence.
- Do not apply global deltas unless multiple large_sector_id values support the same direction.
- Prefer sector_specific or canonical_archetype_specific shadow profiles.
- Positive score promotion requires non-price evidence and clean 180D MFE/MAE.
- 4B rows are overlay/risk calibration only.
- 4C rows are thesis-break/protection calibration only.
- price-only rows cannot promote Stage2/Stage3.
- If a v12 MD weakens an already applied axis, log it as residual counterexample rather than immediately reverting.
- Production scoring must not change unless the user explicitly asks for another promotion batch.

### Expected repository tasks

1. Parse case / trigger / score_simulation / shadow_weight / residual_contribution rows.
2. Validate stock-web price source fields.
3. Validate large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
4. Validate novelty and reuse fields.
5. Deduplicate same_entry_group_id and reused cases.
6. Aggregate by large_sector_id and canonical_archetype_id.
7. Update sector_shadow_profile and archetype_shadow_profile only.
8. Preserve global calibrated profile unless explicitly promoted.
9. Report new independent cases, counterexamples, and residual error types.
10. Add tests that duplicate low-value loops cannot change weights.

### Expected output

- Concise implementation summary.
- Rows accepted/rejected.
- New sector/canonical archetype coverage.
- Existing axis strengthened/weakened/kept.
- No investment recommendation language.

## 28. Source Notes

This review uses stock-web metadata plus the locally generated v12 residual MD corpus. It does not fetch current market candidates or create a live watchlist. All quantitative claims inherit stock-web OHLC rows from the underlying v12 MD trigger rows.
